{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{camp__common_8h_af6a258d8f3ee5206d682d799316314b1}{bool}} rxn\+\_\+condensed\+\_\+phase\+\_\+photolysis\+\_\+update\+\_\+data (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{update\+\_\+data,  }\item[{int \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{rxn\+\_\+int\+\_\+data,  }\item[{double \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{rxn\+\_\+float\+\_\+data,  }\item[{double \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{rxn\+\_\+env\+\_\+data }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Update reaction data. 

Photolysis reactions can have their base (pre-\/scaling) rate constants updated from the host model based on the calculations of an external photolysis module. The structure of the update data is\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{int}} photo\+\_\+id (Id of one or more photolysis reactions set by the host model using the camp\+\_\+rxn\+\_\+photolysis\+::rxn\+\_\+photolysis\+\_\+t\+::set\+\_\+photo\+\_\+id function prior to initializing the solver.)
\item {\bfseries{double}} rate\+\_\+const (New pre-\/scaling rate constant.)
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em update\+\_\+data} & Pointer to the updated reaction data \\
\hline
{\em rxn\+\_\+int\+\_\+data} & Pointer to the reaction integer data \\
\hline
{\em rxn\+\_\+float\+\_\+data} & Pointer to the reaction floating-\/point data \\
\hline
{\em rxn\+\_\+env\+\_\+data} & Pointer to the environment-\/dependent data \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Flag indicating whether this is the reaction to update 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{rxn\_first\_order\_loss\_update\_data@{rxn\_first\_order\_loss\_update\_data}!rxns.h@{rxns.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{rxn\_first\_order\_loss\_update\_data()}{rxn\_first\_order\_loss\_update\_data()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{camp__common_8h_af6a258d8f3ee5206d682d799316314b1}{bool}} rxn\+\_\+first\+\_\+order\+\_\+loss\+\_\+update\+\_\+data (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{update\+\_\+data,  }\item[{int \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{rxn\+\_\+int\+\_\+data,  }\item[{double \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{rxn\+\_\+float\+\_\+data,  }\item[{double \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{rxn\+\_\+env\+\_\+data }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Update reaction data. 

First-\/\+Order loss reactions can have their base (pre-\/scaling) rate constants updated from the host model based on the calculations of an external module. The structure of the update data is\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{int}} rxn\+\_\+id (Id of one or more first-\/order loss reactions set by the host model using the {\ttfamily camp\+\_\+rxn\+\_\+first\+\_\+order\+\_\+loss\+::rxn\+\_\+first\+\_\+order\+\_\+loss\+\_\+t\+::set\+\_\+rxn\+\_\+id} function prior to initializing the solver.)
\item {\bfseries{double}} rate\+\_\+const (New pre-\/scaling rate constant.)
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em update\+\_\+data} & Pointer to the updated reaction data \\
\hline
{\em rxn\+\_\+int\+\_\+data} & Pointer to the reaction integer data \\
\hline
{\em rxn\+\_\+float\+\_\+data} & Pointer to the reaction floating-\/point data \\
\hline
{\em rxn\+\_\+env\+\_\+data} & Pointer to the environment-\/dependent data \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Flag indicating whether this is the reaction to update 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{rxns_8h_a6a060bc8fc2eedb3117ad3c8a768c880}\label{rxns_8h_a6a060bc8fc2eedb3117ad3c8a768c880} 
\index{rxns.h@{rxns.h}!rxn\_photolysis\_update\_data@{rxn\_photolysis\_update\_data}}
\index{rxn\_photolysis\_update\_data@{rxn\_photolysis\_update\_data}!rxns.h@{rxns.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{rxn\_photolysis\_update\_data()}{rxn\_photolysis\_update\_data()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{camp__common_8h_af6a258d8f3ee5206d682d799316314b1}{bool}} rxn\+\_\+photolysis\+\_\+update\+\_\+data (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{update\+\_\+data,  }\item[{int \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{rxn\+\_\+int\+\_\+data,  }\item[{double \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{rxn\+\_\+float\+\_\+data,  }\item[{double \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{rxn\+\_\+env\+\_\+data }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Update reaction data. 

Photolysis reactions can have their base (pre-\/scaling) rate constants updated from the host model based on the calculations of an external photolysis module. The structure of the update data is\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{int}} photo\+\_\+id (Id of one or more photolysis reactions set by the host model using the camp\+\_\+rxn\+\_\+photolysis\+::rxn\+\_\+photolysis\+\_\+t\+::set\+\_\+photo\+\_\+id function prior to initializing the solver.)
\item {\bfseries{double}} rate\+\_\+const (New pre-\/scaling rate constant.)
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em update\+\_\+data} & Pointer to the updated reaction data \\
\hline
{\em rxn\+\_\+int\+\_\+data} & Pointer to the reaction integer data \\
\hline
{\em rxn\+\_\+float\+\_\+data} & Pointer to the reaction floating-\/point data \\
\hline
{\em rxn\+\_\+env\+\_\+data} & Pointer to the environment-\/dependent data \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Flag indicating whether this is the reaction to update 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{rxn\_wet\_deposition\_update\_data@{rxn\_wet\_deposition\_update\_data}!rxns.h@{rxns.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{rxn\_wet\_deposition\_update\_data()}{rxn\_wet\_deposition\_update\_data()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{camp__common_8h_af6a258d8f3ee5206d682d799316314b1}{bool}} rxn\+\_\+wet\+\_\+deposition\+\_\+update\+\_\+data (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{update\+\_\+data,  }\item[{int \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{rxn\+\_\+int\+\_\+data,  }\item[{double \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{rxn\+\_\+float\+\_\+data,  }\item[{double \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{rxn\+\_\+env\+\_\+data }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Update reaction data. 

Wet deposition reactions can have their base (pre-\/scaling) rate constants updated from the host model based on the calculations of an external module. The structure of the update data is\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{int}} rxn\+\_\+id (Id of one or more wet deposition reactions set by the host model using the {\ttfamily camp\+\_\+rxn\+\_\+wet\+\_\+deposition\+::rxn\+\_\+wet\+\_\+deposition\+\_\+t\+::set\+\_\+rxn\+\_\+id} function prior to initializing the solver.)
\item {\bfseries{double}} rate\+\_\+const (New pre-\/scaling rate constant.)
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em update\+\_\+data} & Pointer to the updated reaction data \\
\hline
{\em rxn\+\_\+int\+\_\+data} & Pointer to the reaction integer data \\
\hline
{\em rxn\+\_\+float\+\_\+data} & Pointer to the reaction floating-\/point data \\
\hline
{\em rxn\+\_\+env\+\_\+data} & Pointer to the environment-\/dependent data \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Flag indicating whether this is the reaction to update 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Update reaction data for new environmental conditions. 

For wet deposition reactions this only involves recalculating the rate constant.
